111// testing

113public class ASTTest extends org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.tests.junit.extension.TestCase { 
114        
115        class CheckPositionsMatcher extends ASTMatcher {
116                
117                public CheckPositionsMatcher() {
118                        // include doc tags
119                        super(true);
120                }
121        
122                private void checkPositions(Object source, Object destination) {
123                        assertTrue(source instanceof ASTNode);
124                        assertTrue(destination instanceof ASTNode);
125                        int startPosition = ((ASTNode)source).getStartPosition();
126                        if (startPosition != -1) {
127                                assertTrue(startPosition == ((ASTNode)destination).getStartPosition());
128                        }
129                        int length = ((ASTNode)source).getLength();
130                        if (length != 0) {
131                                assertTrue(length == ((ASTNode)destination).getLength());
132                        }
133                }
134        
135        
136                /**
137                 * @see org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.ASTMatcher#match(AnonymousClassDeclaration, Object)
138                 */
139                public boolean match(AnonymousClassDeclaration node, Object other) {
140                        checkPositions(node, other);
141                        return super.match(node, other);
142                }
143

749        /** @deprecated using deprecated code */
750        public static Test suite() {
751                // TODO (frederic) use buildList + setAstLevel(init) instead...
752                junit.framework.TestSuite suite = new junit.framework.TestSuite(ASTTest.class.getName());
753                
754                Class c = ASTTest.class;
755                Method[] methods = c.getMethods();
756                for (int i = 0, max = methods.length; i < max; i++) {
757                        if (methods[i].getName().startsWith("test")) { //$NON-NLS-1$
758                                suite.addTest(new ASTTest(methods[i].getName(), AST.JLS2));
759                                suite.addTest(new ASTTest(methods[i].getName(), AST.JLS3));
760                        }
761                }
762                return suite;
763        }        
764        
765        AST ast;
766        int API_LEVEL;
767        
768        
769        public ASTTest(String name, int apiLevel) {
770                super(name);
771                this.API_LEVEL = apiLevel;
772        }
773        
774        protected void setUp() throws Exception {
775                super.setUp();
776                ast = AST.newAST(this.API_LEVEL);
777        }
778        
779        protected void tearDown() throws Exception {
780                ast = null;
781                super.tearDown();
782        }
783        
784        /** @deprecated using deprecated code */
785        public String getName() {
786                String name = super.getName();
787                switch (this.API_LEVEL) {
788                        case AST.JLS2:
789                                name = "JLS2 - " + name;
790                                break;
791                        case AST.JLS3:
792                                name = "JLS3 - " + name; 
793                                break;
794                }
795                return name;
796        }
797        
798        /**
799         * Snippets that show how to...
800         * @deprecated using deprecated code
801         */
802        public void testExampleSnippets() {
803                {
804                        AST localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
805                        JavaScriptUnit cu = localAst.newJavaScriptUnit();
806 
807                        // package com.example;
808                        PackageDeclaration pd = localAst.newPackageDeclaration();
809                        pd.setName(localAst.newName(new String[]{"com", "example"})); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
810                        cu.setPackage(pd);
811                        assertTrue(pd.getRoot() == cu);
812 
813                        // import java.io;*;
814                        ImportDeclaration im1 = localAst.newImportDeclaration();
815                        im1.setName(localAst.newName(new String[]{"java", "io"})); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
816                        im1.setOnDemand(true);
817                        cu.imports().add(im1);
818                        assertTrue(im1.getRoot() == cu);
819                        
820                        // import java.util.List;
821                        ImportDeclaration im2 = localAst.newImportDeclaration();
822                        im2.setName(localAst.newName(new String[]{"java", "util", "List"})); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
823                        im2.setOnDemand(false);
824                        cu.imports().add(im2);
825                        assertTrue(im2.getRoot() == cu);
826                        
827                        // /** Spec. \n @deprecated Use {@link #foo() bar} instead. */public class MyClass {}
828                        TypeDeclaration td = localAst.newTypeDeclaration();
829                        if (ast.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2) {
830                                td.setModifiers(Modifier.PUBLIC);
831                        } else {
832                                td.modifiers().add(localAst.newModifier(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD));
833                        }
834                        td.setInterface(false); 
835                        td.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("MyClass")); //$NON-NLS-1$
836                        { 
837                                JSdoc jd = localAst.newJSdoc();
838                                TagElement tg0 = localAst.newTagElement();
839                                jd.tags().add(tg0);
840                                TextElement tx1 = localAst.newTextElement();
841                                tx1.setText("Spec."); //$NON-NLS-1$
842                                tg0.fragments().add(tx1);
843                                TagElement tg1 = localAst.newTagElement();
844                                tg1.setTagName(TagElement.TAG_DEPRECATED);
845                                jd.tags().add(tg1);
846                                TextElement tx2 = localAst.newTextElement();
847                                tx2.setText("Use "); //$NON-NLS-1$
848                                tg1.fragments().add(tx2);
849                                TagElement tg2 = localAst.newTagElement();
850                                tg2.setTagName(TagElement.TAG_LINK);
851                                tg1.fragments().add(tg2);
852                                FunctionRef mr1 = localAst.newFunctionRef();
853                                mr1.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("foo"));
854                                tg2.fragments().add(mr1);
855                                TextElement tx3 = localAst.newTextElement();
856                                tx3.setText("bar"); //$NON-NLS-1$
857                                tg2.fragments().add(tx3);
858                                TextElement tx4 = localAst.newTextElement();
859                                tx2.setText(" instead."); //$NON-NLS-1$
860                                tg1.fragments().add(tx4);
861                        }
862                        
863                        cu.types().add(td);
864                        assertTrue(td.getRoot() == cu);
865                        
866                        // private static boolean DEBUG = true;
867                        VariableDeclarationFragment f1 = localAst.newVariableDeclarationFragment();
868                        f1.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("DEBUG")); //$NON-NLS-1$
869                        f1.setInitializer(localAst.newBooleanLiteral(true));
870                        FieldDeclaration fd = localAst.newFieldDeclaration(f1);
871                        fd.setType(localAst.newPrimitiveType(PrimitiveType.BOOLEAN));
872                        if (ast.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2) {
873                                fd.setModifiers(Modifier.PRIVATE | Modifier.FINAL);
874                        } else {
875                                fd.modifiers().add(localAst.newModifier(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PRIVATE_KEYWORD));
876                                fd.modifiers().add(localAst.newModifier(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STATIC_KEYWORD));
877                        }
878                        td.bodyDeclarations().add(fd);
879                        assertTrue(fd.getRoot() == cu);
880                        
881                        // public static void main();
882                        FunctionDeclaration md = localAst.newFunctionDeclaration();
883                        if (ast.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2) {
884                                md.setModifiers(Modifier.PUBLIC | Modifier.STATIC);
885                                md.setReturnType(localAst.newPrimitiveType(PrimitiveType.VOID));
886                        } else {
887                                md.modifiers().add(localAst.newModifier(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD));
888                                md.modifiers().add(localAst.newModifier(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STATIC_KEYWORD));
889                                md.setReturnType2(localAst.newPrimitiveType(PrimitiveType.VOID));
890                        }
891                        md.setConstructor(false);
892                        md.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("main")); //$NON-NLS-1$
893                        td.bodyDeclarations().add(md);
894                        assertTrue(md.getRoot() == cu);
895                        
896                        // String[] args
897                        SingleVariableDeclaration a1 = localAst.newSingleVariableDeclaration();
898                        a1.setType(localAst.newArrayType(
899                                localAst.newSimpleType(localAst.newSimpleName("String")))); //$NON-NLS-1$
900                        a1.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("args")); //$NON-NLS-1$
901                        md.parameters().add(a1);
902                        assertTrue(a1.getRoot() == cu);
903                        
904                        // {}
905                        Block b = localAst.newBlock();
906                        md.setBody(b);
907                        assertTrue(b.getRoot() == cu);
908 
909                        // System.out.println("hello world");                
910                        FunctionInvocation e = localAst.newFunctionInvocation();
911                        e.setExpression(localAst.newName(new String[] {"System", "out"})); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
912                        e.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("println")); //$NON-NLS-1$
913                        StringLiteral h = localAst.newStringLiteral();
914                        h.setLiteralValue("hello world"); //$NON-NLS-1$
915                        e.arguments().add(h);
916                        
917                        b.statements().add(localAst.newExpressionStatement(e));
918                        assertTrue(e.getRoot() == cu);
919                        assertTrue(h.getRoot() == cu);
920                        
921                        // new String[len];
922                        ArrayCreation ac1 = localAst.newArrayCreation();
923                        ac1.setType(
924                                localAst.newArrayType(
925                                        localAst.newSimpleType(localAst.newSimpleName("String")))); //$NON-NLS-1$
926                        ac1.dimensions().add(localAst.newSimpleName("len")); //$NON-NLS-1$
927                        b.statements().add(localAst.newExpressionStatement(ac1));
928                        assertTrue(ac1.getRoot() == cu);
929 
930                        // new double[7][24][];
931                        ArrayCreation ac2 = localAst.newArrayCreation();
932                        ac2.setType(
933                                localAst.newArrayType(
934                                        localAst.newPrimitiveType(PrimitiveType.DOUBLE), 3));
935                        ac2.dimensions().add(localAst.newNumberLiteral("7")); //$NON-NLS-1$
936                        ac2.dimensions().add(localAst.newNumberLiteral("24")); //$NON-NLS-1$
937                        b.statements().add(localAst.newExpressionStatement(ac2));
938                        assertTrue(ac2.getRoot() == cu);
939 
940                        // new int[] {1, 2};
941                        ArrayCreation ac3 = localAst.newArrayCreation();
942                        ac3.setType(
943                                localAst.newArrayType(
944                                        localAst.newPrimitiveType(PrimitiveType.INT)));
945                        ArrayInitializer ai = localAst.newArrayInitializer();
946                        ac3.setInitializer(ai);
947                        ai.expressions().add(localAst.newNumberLiteral("1")); //$NON-NLS-1$
948                        ai.expressions().add(localAst.newNumberLiteral("2")); //$NON-NLS-1$
949                        b.statements().add(localAst.newExpressionStatement(ac3));
950                        assertTrue(ac3.getRoot() == cu);
951                        assertTrue(ai.getRoot() == cu);
952                        
953                        // new String(10);
954                        ClassInstanceCreation cr1 = localAst.newClassInstanceCreation();
955                        if (ast.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2) {
956                                cr1.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("String")); //$NON-NLS-1$
957                        } else {
958                                cr1.setType(localAst.newSimpleType(localAst.newSimpleName("String"))); //$NON-NLS-1$
959                        }
960                        cr1.arguments().add(localAst.newNumberLiteral("10"));                 //$NON-NLS-1$
961                        b.statements().add(localAst.newExpressionStatement(cr1));
962                        assertTrue(cr1.getRoot() == cu);
963 
964                        // new Listener() {public void handleEvent() {} };
965                        ClassInstanceCreation cr2 = localAst.newClassInstanceCreation();
966                        AnonymousClassDeclaration ad1 = localAst.newAnonymousClassDeclaration();
967                        cr2.setAnonymousClassDeclaration(ad1);
968                        if (ast.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2) {
969                                cr2.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("Listener")); //$NON-NLS-1$
970                        } else {
971                                cr2.setType(localAst.newSimpleType(localAst.newSimpleName("Listener"))); //$NON-NLS-1$
972                        }
973                        FunctionDeclaration md0 = localAst.newFunctionDeclaration();
974                        if (ast.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2) {
975                                md0.setModifiers(Modifier.PUBLIC);
976                        } else {
977                                md0.modifiers().add(localAst.newModifier(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD));
978                        }
979                        md0.setName(localAst.newSimpleName("handleEvent")); //$NON-NLS-1$
980                        md0.setBody(localAst.newBlock());
981                        ad1.bodyDeclarations().add(md0);
982                        b.statements().add(localAst.newExpressionStatement(cr2));
983                        assertTrue(cr2.getRoot() == cu);
984                        assertTrue(md0.getRoot() == cu);
985                        assertTrue(ad1.getRoot() == cu);
986 
987                }
988        }
989        
990        abstract class Property {
991                
992                /**
993                 * Indicates whether this property is compulsory, in that every node
994                 * must have a value at all times.
995                 */
996                private boolean compulsory;
997 
998                private Class nodeType;                
999                private String propertyName;
1000 
1001                /**
1002                 * Creates a new property with the given name.
1003                 */
1004                Property(String propertyName, boolean compulsory, Class nodeType) {
1005                        this.propertyName = propertyName;
1006                        this.compulsory = compulsory;
1007                        this.nodeType = nodeType;
1008                }

1011                 * Returns a sample node of a type suitable for storing
1012                 * in this property.

1015                 * @param parented <code>true</code> if the sample should be
1016                 *    parented, and <code>false</code> if unparented
1017                 * @return a sample node
1018                 */
1019                public abstract ASTNode sample(AST targetAST, boolean parented);
1020

1031                 */
1032                public ASTNode[] counterExamples(AST targetAST) {
1033                        return new ASTNode[] {};
1034                }

1036                /**
1037                 * Returns a sample node of a type suitable for storing
1038                 * in this property. The sample embeds the node itself.
1039                 * <p>
1040                 * For instance, for an Expression-valued property of a given
1041                 * Statement, this method returns an Expression that embeds
1042                 * this Statement node (as a descendent).
1043                 * </p>
1044                 * <p>
1045                 * Returns <code>null</code> if such an embedding is impossible.
1046                 * For instance, for an Name-valued property of a given
1047                 * Statement, this method returns <code>null</code> because
1048                 * an Expression cannot be embedded in a Name.
1049                 * </p>
1050                 * <p>
1051                 * This implementation returns <code>null</code>. Subclasses
1052                 * should reimplement to specify an embedding.
1053                 * </p>
1054                 * 
1055                 * @return a sample node that embeds the given node,
1056                 *    and <code>null</code> if such an embedding is impossible
1057                 */
1058                public ASTNode wrap() {
1059                        return null;
1060                }
1061                
1062                /**
1063                 * Undoes the effects of a previous <code>wrap</code>.
1064                 * <p>
1065                 * This implementation does nothing. Subclasses
1066                 * should reimplement if they reimplement <code>wrap</code>.
1067                 * </p>
1068                 */
1069                public void unwrap() {
1070                }

1101                 * </p>
1102                 *

1104                 */
1105                public void set(ASTNode value) {

1114        /**
1115         * Exercises the given property of the given node.
1116         * 
1117         * @param node the node to test
1118         * @param prop the property descriptor
1119         */
1120        void genericPropertyTest(ASTNode node, Property prop) {
1121                
1122                ASTNode x1 = prop.sample(node.getAST(), false);
1123                prop.set(x1);
1124                assertTrue(prop.get() == x1);
1125                assertTrue(x1.getParent() == node);
1126                
1127                // check handling of null
1128                if (prop.isCompulsory()) {
1129                        try {
1130                                prop.set(null);
1131                                assertTrue(false);
1132                        } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1133                                // pass
1134                        }
1135                } else {
1136                        long previousCount = node.getAST().modificationCount();
1137                        prop.set(null);
1138                        assertTrue(prop.get() == null);
1139                        assertTrue(node.getAST().modificationCount() > previousCount);
1140                }                        
1141 
1142                // check that a child from a different AST is detected
1143                try {
1144                        AST newAST = AST.newAST(node.getAST().apiLevel());
1145                        prop.set(prop.sample(newAST, false));
1146                        assertTrue(false);
1147                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1148                        // pass
1149                }
1150 
1151                // check that a child with a parent is detected
1152                try {
1153                        ASTNode b1 = prop.sample(node.getAST(), true);
1154                        prop.set(b1); // bogus: already has parent
1155                        assertTrue(false);
1156                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1157                        // pass
1158                }
1159 
1160                // check that a cycle is detected
1161                assertTrue(node.getParent() == null);
1162                ASTNode s1 = null;
1163                try {
1164                        s1 = prop.wrap();
1165                        if (s1 != null) {
1166                                prop.set(s1);  // bogus: creates a cycle
1167                                assertTrue(false);
1168                        }
1169                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1170                        // pass
1171                } finally {
1172                        if (s1 != null) {
1173                                prop.unwrap();
1174                                assertTrue(node.getParent() == null);
1175                        }
1176                }
1177                
1178                // check that a child of the wrong type is detected
1179                ASTNode b1[] = prop.counterExamples(node.getAST());
1180                for (int i = 0; i < b1.length; i++) {
1181                        try {
1182                                prop.set(b1[i]); // bogus: wrong type
1183                                assertTrue(false);
1184                        } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1185                                // pass
1186                        }
1187                }
1188 
1189        }
1190 
1191        /**
1192         * Exercises the given property of the given node.
1193         * 
1194         * @param node the node to test
1195         * @param children the node to test
1196         * @param prop the property descriptor
1197         */
1198        void genericPropertyListTest(ASTNode node, List children, Property prop) {
1199                
1200                // wipe the slate clean
1201                children.clear();
1202                assertTrue(children.size() == 0);
1203                
1204                // add a child
1205                ASTNode x1 = prop.sample(node.getAST(), false);
1206                long previousCount = node.getAST().modificationCount();
1207                children.add(x1);
1208                assertTrue(node.getAST().modificationCount() > previousCount);
1209                assertTrue(children.size() == 1);
1210                assertTrue(children.get(0) == x1);
1211                assertTrue(x1.getParent() == node);
1212                
1213                // add a second child
1214                ASTNode x2 = prop.sample(node.getAST(), false);
1215                previousCount = node.getAST().modificationCount();
1216                children.add(x2);
1217                assertTrue(node.getAST().modificationCount() > previousCount);
1218                assertTrue(children.size() == 2);
1219                assertTrue(children.get(0) == x1);
1220                assertTrue(children.get(1) == x2);
1221                assertTrue(x1.getParent() == node);
1222                assertTrue(x2.getParent() == node);
1223 
1224                // remove the first child
1225                previousCount = node.getAST().modificationCount();
1226                children.remove(0);
1227                assertTrue(node.getAST().modificationCount() > previousCount);
1228                assertTrue(children.size() == 1);
1229                assertTrue(children.get(0) == x2);
1230                assertTrue(x1.getParent() == null);
1231                assertTrue(x2.getParent() == node);
1232 
1233                // remove the remaining child
1234                previousCount = node.getAST().modificationCount();
1235                children.remove(x2);
1236                assertTrue(node.getAST().modificationCount() > previousCount);
1237                assertTrue(children.size() == 0);
1238                assertTrue(x1.getParent() == null);
1239                assertTrue(x2.getParent() == null);
1240 
1241                // check that null is never allowed
1242                try {
1243                        children.add(null);
1244                        assertTrue(false);
1245                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1246                        // pass
1247                }
1248 
1249                // check that a child from a different AST is detected
1250                try {
1251                        AST newAST = AST.newAST(node.getAST().apiLevel());
1252                        children.add(prop.sample(newAST, false));
1253                        assertTrue(false);
1254                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1255                        // pass
1256                }
1257 
1258                // check that a child with a parent is detected
1259                try {
1260                        ASTNode b1 = prop.sample(node.getAST(), true);
1261                        children.add(b1); // bogus: already has parent
1262                        assertTrue(false);
1263                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1264                        // pass
1265                }
1266 
1267                // check that a cycle is detected
1268                assertTrue(node.getParent() == null);
1269                ASTNode s1 = null;
1270                try {
1271                        s1 = prop.wrap();
1272                        if (s1 != null) {
1273                                children.add(s1);  // bogus: creates a cycle
1274                                assertTrue(false);
1275                        }
1276                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1277                        // pass
1278                } finally {
1279                        if (s1 != null) {
1280                                prop.unwrap();
1281                                assertTrue(node.getParent() == null);
1282                        }
1283                }
1284                
1285                // check that a child of the wrong type is detected
1286                ASTNode b1[] = prop.counterExamples(node.getAST());
1287                for (int i = 0; i < b1.length; i++) {
1288                        try {
1289                                children.add(b1[i]); // bogus: wrong type
1290                                assertTrue(false);
1291                        } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1292                                // pass
1293                        }
1294                }
1295                
1296        }

1298        /** @deprecated using deprecated code */
1299        public void testAST() {
1300                
1301                assertTrue(AST.JLS2 == 2);
1302                assertTrue(AST.JLS3 == 3);
1303                
1304                AST a0 = new AST(); // deprecated, but still 2.0
1305                assertTrue(a0.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2);
1306                AST a1 = new AST(new HashMap()); // deprecated, but still 2.0
1307                assertTrue(a1.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2);
1308                AST a2 = AST.newAST(AST.JLS2);
1309                assertTrue(a2.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2);
1310                AST a3 = AST.newAST(AST.JLS3);
1311                assertTrue(a3.apiLevel() == AST.JLS3);
1312                
1313                
1314                // modification count is always non-negative
1315                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() >= 0);
1316                
1317                // modification count increases for node creations
1318                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1319                SimpleName x = ast.newSimpleName("first"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1320                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1321 
1322                // modification count does not increase for reading node attributes
1323                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1324                x.getIdentifier();
1325                x.getParent();
1326                x.getRoot();
1327                x.getAST();
1328                x.getFlags();
1329                x.getStartPosition();
1330                x.getLength();
1331                x.equals(x);
1332                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1333 
1334                // modification count does not increase for reading or writing properties
1335                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1336                x.getProperty("any"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1337                x.setProperty("any", "value"); // N.B. //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
1338                x.properties();
1339                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1340 
1341                // modification count increases for changing node attributes
1342                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1343                x.setIdentifier("second"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1344                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1345                
1346                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1347                x.setFlags(0);
1348                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1349                
1350                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1351                x.setSourceRange(-1,0);
1352                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1353        }

1355        public void testWellKnownBindings() {

1370                        "java.io.Serializable", //$NON-NLS-1$

1372                        "java.lang.Byte", //$NON-NLS-1$
1373                        "java.lang.Character", //$NON-NLS-1$

1375                        "java.lang.Float", //$NON-NLS-1$

1392                }

1395                for (int i = 0; i<nwkbs.length; i++) {
1396                        assertTrue(ast.resolveWellKnownType(nwkbs[i]) == null);
1397                }

1400        public void testSimpleName() {
1401                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1402                SimpleName x = ast.newSimpleName("foo"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1403                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1404                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1405                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
1406                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
1407                assertTrue("foo".equals(x.getIdentifier())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1408                assertTrue("foo".equals(x.getFullyQualifiedName())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1409                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.SIMPLE_NAME);
1410                assertTrue(x.isDeclaration() == false);
1411                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == SimpleName.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
1412                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
1413                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1414 
1415                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1416                x.setIdentifier("bar"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1417                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1418                assertTrue("bar".equals(x.getIdentifier())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1419                assertTrue("bar".equals(x.getFullyQualifiedName())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1420 
1421                // check that property cannot be set to null
1422                try {
1423                        x.setIdentifier(null);
1424                        assertTrue(false);
1425                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1426                        // pass
1427                }
1428                
1429                // check that property cannot be set to keyword or reserved work
1430                String[] reserved  = 
1431                                new String[] {
1432                                                "true", "false", "null", // literals //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
1433                                                "abstract", "default", "if", "private", "this", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$ //$NON-NLS-5$
1434                                                "boolean", "do", "implements", "protected", "throw", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$ //$NON-NLS-5$
1435                                                "break", "double", "import", "public", "throws", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$ //$NON-NLS-5$

1509        public void testQualifiedName() {
1510                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1511                final QualifiedName x = ast.newQualifiedName(
1512                        ast.newSimpleName("q"), //$NON-NLS-1$
1513                        ast.newSimpleName("i")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1514                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1515                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1516                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
1517                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
1518                assertTrue(x.getQualifier().getParent() == x);
1519                assertTrue(x.getName().getParent() == x);
1520                assertTrue(x.getName().isDeclaration() == false);
1521                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.QUALIFIED_NAME);
1522                assertTrue("q.i".equals(x.getFullyQualifiedName())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1523                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == QualifiedName.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
1524                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
1525                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1526 
1527                genericPropertyTest(x, new Property("Qualifier", true, Name.class) { //$NON-NLS-1$
1528                        public ASTNode sample(AST targetAst, boolean parented) {
1529                                QualifiedName result = targetAst.newQualifiedName(
1530                                        targetAst.newSimpleName("a"), //$NON-NLS-1$
1531                                        targetAst.newSimpleName("b")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1532                                if (parented) {
1533                                        targetAst.newExpressionStatement(result);
1534                                }
1535                                return result;
1536                        }
1537                        public ASTNode wrap() {
1538                                QualifiedName s1 = ast.newQualifiedName(x, ast.newSimpleName("z")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1539                                return s1;
1540                        }
1541                        public void unwrap() {
1542                                QualifiedName s1 = (QualifiedName) x.getParent();
1543                                s1.setQualifier(ast.newSimpleName("z")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1544                        }
1545                        public ASTNode get() {
1546                                return x.getQualifier();
1547                        }
1548                        public void set(ASTNode value) {
1549                                x.setQualifier((Name) value);
1550                        }
1551                });
1552

1555                                SimpleName result = targetAst.newSimpleName("foo"); //$NON-NLS-1$

1557                                        targetAst.newExpressionStatement(result);

1575        public void testNameFactories() {
1576                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1577                Name x = ast.newName("foo"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1578                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1579                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();

1581                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
1582                assertTrue("foo".equals(x.getFullyQualifiedName())); //$NON-NLS-1$

1584 
1585                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1586                x = ast.newName("foo.bar"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1587                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1588                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1589                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
1590                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
1591                assertTrue("foo.bar".equals(x.getFullyQualifiedName())); //$NON-NLS-1$

1640        public void testBooleanLiteral() {
1641                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1642                BooleanLiteral x = ast.newBooleanLiteral(true);
1643                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1644                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1645                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
1646                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
1647                assertTrue(x.booleanValue() == true);
1648                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.BOOLEAN_LITERAL);
1649                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == BooleanLiteral.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
1650                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
1651                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1652                
1653                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1654                x.setBooleanValue(false);
1655                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1656                assertTrue(x.booleanValue() == false);
1657                
1658                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1659                x.setBooleanValue(true);
1660                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1661                assertTrue(x.booleanValue() == true);
1662        }

1664        public void testStringLiteral() {
1665                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1666                // check 0-arg factory first
1667                StringLiteral x = ast.newStringLiteral();
1668                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1669                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1670                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
1671                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
1672                assertTrue("\"\"".equals(x.getEscapedValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1673                assertTrue("".equals(x.getLiteralValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1674                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.STRING_LITERAL);
1675                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == StringLiteral.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
1676                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
1677                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1678                
1679                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1680                x.setEscapedValue("\"bye\""); //$NON-NLS-1$
1681                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1682                assertTrue("\"bye\"".equals(x.getEscapedValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1683                assertTrue("bye".equals(x.getLiteralValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1684 
1685                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1686                x.setLiteralValue("hi"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1687                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1688                assertTrue("\"hi\"".equals(x.getEscapedValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1689                assertTrue("hi".equals(x.getLiteralValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1690 
1691                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1692                x.setLiteralValue("\\012\\015"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1693                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1694                assertEquals("different", "\"\\\\012\\\\015\"", x.getEscapedValue()); //$NON-NLS-1$
1695                assertTrue("\\012\\015".equals(x.getLiteralValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1696 
1697                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1698                x.setLiteralValue("\012\015"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1699                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1700                assertTrue("\n\r".equals(x.getLiteralValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1701                assertEquals("different", "\"\\n\\r\"", x.getEscapedValue()); //$NON-NLS-1$
1702 
1703                // check that property cannot be set to null
1704                try {
1705                        x.setEscapedValue(null);
1706                        assertTrue(false);
1707                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1708                        // pass
1709                }
1710 
1711                // check that property cannot be set to null
1712                try {
1713                        x.setLiteralValue(null);
1714                        assertTrue(false);
1715                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1716                        // pass
1717                }
1718        }

1720        public void testStringLiteralUnicode() {
1721                AST localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
1722                StringLiteral literal = localAst.newStringLiteral();
1723                literal.setEscapedValue("\"hello\\u0026\\u0050worl\\u0064\""); //$NON-NLS-1$
1724                assertTrue(literal.getLiteralValue().equals("hello&Pworld")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1725                
1726                localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
1727                literal = localAst.newStringLiteral();
1728                literal.setEscapedValue("\"hello\\nworld\""); //$NON-NLS-1$
1729                assertTrue(literal.getLiteralValue().equals("hello\nworld")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1730                
1731                localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
1732                literal = localAst.newStringLiteral();
1733                literal.setLiteralValue("hello\nworld"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1734                assertTrue(literal.getLiteralValue().equals("hello\nworld")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1735                
1736                localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
1737                literal = localAst.newStringLiteral();
1738                literal.setLiteralValue("\n"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1739                assertTrue(literal.getEscapedValue().equals("\"\\n\"")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1740                assertTrue(literal.getLiteralValue().equals("\n")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1741                
1742                localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
1743                literal = localAst.newStringLiteral();
1744                literal.setEscapedValue("\"hello\\\"world\""); //$NON-NLS-1$
1745                assertTrue(literal.getLiteralValue().equals("hello\"world")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1746                
1747                localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
1748                literal = localAst.newStringLiteral();
1749                literal.setLiteralValue("hello\\u0026world"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1750                assertTrue(literal.getLiteralValue().equals("hello\\u0026world")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1751                
1752                localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
1753                literal = localAst.newStringLiteral();
1754                literal.setLiteralValue("hello\\u0026world"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1755                assertTrue(literal.getEscapedValue().equals("\"hello\\\\u0026world\"")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1756                
1757                localAst = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
1758                literal = localAst.newStringLiteral();
1759                literal.setLiteralValue("\\u0001"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1760                assertTrue(literal.getEscapedValue().equals("\"\\\\u0001\"")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1761        }

1763        public void testCharacterLiteral() {
1764                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1765                CharacterLiteral x = ast.newCharacterLiteral();
1766                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1767                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1768                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
1769                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
1770                assertTrue(x.getEscapedValue().startsWith("\'")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1771                assertTrue(x.getEscapedValue().endsWith("\'")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1772                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.CHARACTER_LITERAL);
1773                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == CharacterLiteral.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
1774                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
1775                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1776 
1777                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1778                x.setEscapedValue("\'z\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1779                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1780                assertTrue("\'z\'".equals(x.getEscapedValue())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1781                assertTrue(x.charValue() == 'z');
1782 
1783                // test other factory method
1784                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1785                CharacterLiteral y = ast.newCharacterLiteral();
1786                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1787                assertTrue(y.getAST() == ast);
1788                assertTrue(y.getParent() == null);
1789                String v = y.getEscapedValue();
1790                assertTrue(v.length() >= 3 && v.charAt(0) == '\'' & v.charAt(v.length()-1 ) == '\'');
1791 
1792                // check that property cannot be set to null
1793                try {
1794                        x.setEscapedValue(null);
1795                        assertTrue(false);
1796                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1797                        // pass
1798                }
1799                
1800                // test escaped characters
1801                // b, t, n, f, r, ", ', \, 0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, or 7
1802                try {
1803                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\b\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1804                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\t\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1805                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\n\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1806                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\f\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1807                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\\"\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1808                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\'\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1809                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\\\\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1810                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\0\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1811                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\1\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1812                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\2\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1813                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\3\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1814                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\4\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1815                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\5\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1816                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\6\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1817                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\7\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1818                        x.setEscapedValue("\'\\u0041\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1819                        assertTrue(x.charValue() == 'A');
1820                } catch(IllegalArgumentException e) {
1821                        assertTrue(false);
1822                }
1823                
1824                x.setCharValue('\u0041');
1825                assertTrue(x.getEscapedValue().equals("\'A\'")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1826                x.setCharValue('\t');
1827                assertTrue(x.getEscapedValue().equals("\'\\t\'")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1828                x.setEscapedValue("\'\\\\\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1829                assertTrue(x.getEscapedValue().equals("\'\\\\\'")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1830                assertTrue(x.charValue() == '\\');
1831                x.setEscapedValue("\'\\\'\'"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1832                assertTrue(x.getEscapedValue().equals("\'\\\'\'")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1833                assertTrue(x.charValue() == '\'');                
1834                x.setCharValue('\'');
1835                assertTrue(x.getEscapedValue().equals("\'\\\'\'")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1836                assertTrue(x.charValue() == '\'');                
1837                x.setCharValue('\\');
1838                assertTrue(x.getEscapedValue().equals("\'\\\\\'")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1839                assertTrue(x.charValue() == '\\');                
1840        }

1842        public void testNumberLiteral() {

1844                NumberLiteral x = ast.newNumberLiteral("1234"); //$NON-NLS-1$
1845                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1846                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();

1849                assertTrue("1234".equals(x.getToken())); //$NON-NLS-1$
1850                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.NUMBER_LITERAL);
1851                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == NumberLiteral.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
1852                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
1853                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1854

1857                NumberLiteral y = ast.newNumberLiteral();
1858                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1859                assertTrue(y.getAST() == ast);
1860                assertTrue(y.getParent() == null);
1861                assertTrue("0".equals(y.getToken())); //$NON-NLS-1$

1863                final String[] samples =
1864                        { "0", "1", "1234567890", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
1865                          "0L", "1L", "1234567890L", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$

1867                          "077", "0177", "012345670", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
1868                          "077L", "0177L", "012345670L", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
1869                          "077l", "0177l", "012345670l", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
1870                          "0x00", "0x1", "0x0123456789ABCDEF", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
1871                          "0x00L", "0x1L", "0x0123456789ABCDEFL", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
1872                          "0x00l", "0x1l", "0x0123456789ABCDEFl", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$
1873                          "1e1f", "2.f", ".3f", "0f", "3.14f", "6.022137e+23f", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$ //$NON-NLS-5$ //$NON-NLS-6$
1874                          "1e1", "2.", ".3", "0.0", "3.14", "1e-9d", "1e137", //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$ //$NON-NLS-5$ //$NON-NLS-6$ //$NON-NLS-7$
1875                        };
1876                for (int i = 0; i < samples.length; i++) {

1878                        x.setToken(samples[i]);
1879                        assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1880                        assertTrue(samples[i].equals(x.getToken()));
1881                }
1882

1884                try {
1885                        x.setToken(null);
1886                        assertTrue(false);
1887                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1888                        // pass
1889                }
1890 
1891        }

1929        public void testPrimitiveType() {
1930                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1931                PrimitiveType x = ast.newPrimitiveType(PrimitiveType.INT);
1932                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1933                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1934                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
1935                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
1936                assertTrue(x.getPrimitiveTypeCode().equals(PrimitiveType.INT));
1937                assertTrue(!x.isSimpleType());
1938                assertTrue(!x.isArrayType());
1939                assertTrue(x.isPrimitiveType());
1940                assertTrue(!x.isParameterizedType());
1941                assertTrue(!x.isQualifiedType());
1942                assertTrue(!x.isWildcardType());
1943                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.PRIMITIVE_TYPE);
1944                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == PrimitiveType.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
1945                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
1946                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
1947                
1948                // check the names of the primitive type codes
1949                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.BYTE.toString().equals("byte")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1950                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.INT.toString().equals("int")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1951                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.BOOLEAN.toString().equals("boolean")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1952                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.CHAR.toString().equals("char")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1953                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.SHORT.toString().equals("short")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1954                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.LONG.toString().equals("long")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1955                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.FLOAT.toString().equals("float")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1956                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.DOUBLE.toString().equals("double")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1957                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.VOID.toString().equals("void")); //$NON-NLS-1$
1958 
1959                
1960                PrimitiveType.Code[] known = {
1961                        PrimitiveType.BOOLEAN,
1962                        PrimitiveType.BYTE,
1963                        PrimitiveType.CHAR,
1964                        PrimitiveType.INT,
1965                        PrimitiveType.SHORT,
1966                        PrimitiveType.LONG,
1967                        PrimitiveType.FLOAT,
1968                        PrimitiveType.DOUBLE,
1969                        PrimitiveType.VOID,
1970                };
1971                
1972                // check all primitive type codes are distinct
1973                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
1974                        for (int j = 0; j < known.length; j++) {
1975                                assertTrue(i == j || !known[i].equals(known[j]));
1976                        }
1977                }
1978 
1979                // check all primitive type codes work
1980                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
1981                        previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
1982                        x.setPrimitiveTypeCode(known[i]);
1983                        assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
1984                        assertTrue(x.getPrimitiveTypeCode().equals(known[i]));
1985                }
1986                // ensure null does not work as a primitive type code
1987                try {
1988                        x.setPrimitiveTypeCode(null);
1989                        assertTrue(false);
1990                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
1991                        // pass
1992                }
1993 
1994                // check toCode lookup of primitive type code by name
1995                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
1996                        String name = known[i].toString();
1997                        assertTrue(PrimitiveType.toCode(name).equals(known[i]));
1998                }
1999                assertTrue(PrimitiveType.toCode("not-a-type") == null); //$NON-NLS-1$
2000        }

2218        public void testWildcardType() {
2219                if (ast.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2) {
2220                        // node type introduced in 3.0 API
2221                        try {
2222                                ast.newWildcardType();
2223                                assertTrue(false);
2224                        } catch (UnsupportedOperationException e) {
2225                                // pass
2226                        }
2227                        return;
2228                }
2229                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
2230                final WildcardType x = ast.newWildcardType();
2231                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
2232                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
2233                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
2234                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
2235                assertTrue(x.getBound() == null);
2236                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == true);
2237                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.WILDCARD_TYPE);
2238                assertTrue(!x.isSimpleType());
2239                assertTrue(!x.isArrayType());
2240                assertTrue(!x.isPrimitiveType());
2241                assertTrue(!x.isParameterizedType());
2242                assertTrue(!x.isQualifiedType());

2244                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == WildcardType.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
2245                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
2246                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
2247

2252                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == false);
2253                x.setUpperBound(true);
2254                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == true);
2255                x.setBound(null);
2256                x.setUpperBound(false);
2257                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == false);
2258                x.setUpperBound(true);
2259                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == true);
2260

2264                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == false);
2265                x.setBound(null, true);
2266                assertTrue(x.getBound() == null);
2267                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == true);
2268                x.setBound(b, true);
2269                assertTrue(x.getBound() == b);
2270                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == true);
2271                x.setBound(null, false);
2272                assertTrue(x.getBound() == null);
2273                assertTrue(x.isUpperBound() == false);

3533        public void testTextElement() {
3534                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
3535                final TextElement x = ast.newTextElement();
3536                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
3537                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
3538                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
3539                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
3540                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.TEXT_ELEMENT);
3541                assertTrue(x.getText().length() == 0);
3542                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == 
3543                        TextElement.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
3544                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
3545                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
3546                
3547                // text property
3548                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
3549                String s1 = new String("hello");
3550                x.setText(s1);
3551                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
3552                assertTrue(x.getText() == s1);
3553                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
3554                String s2 = new String("");
3555                x.setText(s2);
3556                assertTrue(x.getText() == s2);
3557                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
3558                // check that property cannot be set to null
3559                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
3560                try {
3561                        x.setText(null);
3562                        assertTrue(false);
3563                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
3564                        // pass
3565                }
3566                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
3567                // check that property cannot include */
3568                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
3569                try {
3570                        x.setText("this would be the */ end of it");  //$NON-NLS-1$
3571                        assertTrue(false);
3572                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
3573                        // pass
3574                }
3575                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
3576        }

4296        
4297        public void testAssignment() {
4298                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
4299                final Assignment x = ast.newAssignment();
4300                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
4301                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
4302                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
4303                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
4304                assertTrue(x.getOperator() == Assignment.Operator.ASSIGN);
4305                assertTrue(x.getLeftHandSide().getParent() == x);
4306                assertTrue(x.getRightHandSide().getParent() == x);
4307                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.ASSIGNMENT);
4308                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == 
4309                        Assignment.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
4310                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
4311                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
4312        
4313                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
4314                x.setOperator(Assignment.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN);
4315                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
4316                assertTrue(x.getOperator() == Assignment.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN);
4317                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN 
4318                        != Assignment.Operator.ASSIGN);
4319 
4320                // check the names of the primitive type codes
4321                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.ASSIGN.toString().equals("=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4322                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN.toString().equals("+=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4323                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.MINUS_ASSIGN.toString().equals("-=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4324                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.TIMES_ASSIGN.toString().equals("*=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4325                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.DIVIDE_ASSIGN.toString().equals("/=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4326                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.REMAINDER_ASSIGN.toString().equals("%=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4327                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.LEFT_SHIFT_ASSIGN.toString().equals("<<=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4328                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.RIGHT_SHIFT_SIGNED_ASSIGN.toString().equals(">>=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4329                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.RIGHT_SHIFT_UNSIGNED_ASSIGN.toString().equals(">>>=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4330                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.BIT_AND_ASSIGN.toString().equals("&=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4331                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.BIT_OR_ASSIGN.toString().equals("|=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4332                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.BIT_XOR_ASSIGN.toString().equals("^=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
4333                
4334                Assignment.Operator[] known = {
4335                        Assignment.Operator.ASSIGN,
4336                        Assignment.Operator.PLUS_ASSIGN,
4337                        Assignment.Operator.MINUS_ASSIGN,
4338                        Assignment.Operator.TIMES_ASSIGN,
4339                        Assignment.Operator.DIVIDE_ASSIGN,
4340                        Assignment.Operator.REMAINDER_ASSIGN,
4341                        Assignment.Operator.LEFT_SHIFT_ASSIGN,
4342                        Assignment.Operator.RIGHT_SHIFT_SIGNED_ASSIGN,
4343                        Assignment.Operator.RIGHT_SHIFT_UNSIGNED_ASSIGN,
4344                        Assignment.Operator.BIT_AND_ASSIGN,
4345                        Assignment.Operator.BIT_OR_ASSIGN,
4346                        Assignment.Operator.BIT_XOR_ASSIGN,
4347                };
4348                
4349                // check all operators are distinct
4350                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
4351                        for (int j = 0; j < known.length; j++) {
4352                                assertTrue(i == j || !known[i].equals(known[j]));
4353                        }
4354                }
4355 
4356                // check all operators work
4357                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
4358                        previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
4359                        x.setOperator(known[i]);
4360                        assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
4361                        assertTrue(x.getOperator().equals(known[i]));
4362                }
4363                // ensure null does not work as a primitive type code
4364                try {
4365                        x.setOperator(null);
4366                        assertTrue(false);
4367                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
4368                        // pass
4369                }
4370 
4371                // check toOperator lookup of operators by name
4372                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
4373                        String name = known[i].toString();
4374                        assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.toOperator(name).equals(known[i]));
4375                }
4376                assertTrue(Assignment.Operator.toOperator("not-an-op") == null); //$NON-NLS-1$
4377

4987        /**
4988         * Exercise the leadingComment property.
4989         * 
4990         * @param x the statement to test
4991         * @deprecated (Uses get/setLeadingComment() which is deprecated)
4992         */
4993        void tLeadingComment(Statement x) {
4994                
4995                // check that null is allowed
4996                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
4997                x.setLeadingComment(null);
4998                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
4999                assertTrue(x.getLeadingComment() == null);
5000                
5001                // check that regular comment is allowed
5002                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
5003                x.setLeadingComment("/* X */"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5004                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
5005                assertTrue(x.getLeadingComment() == "/* X */"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5006                
5007                // check that regular comment with line breaks is allowed
5008                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
5009                x.setLeadingComment("/* X\n *Y\n */"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5010                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
5011                assertTrue(x.getLeadingComment() == "/* X\n *Y\n */"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5012                
5013                // check that end-of-line comment is allowed
5014                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
5015                x.setLeadingComment("// X\n"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5016                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
5017                assertTrue(x.getLeadingComment() == "// X\n"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5018 
5019                // check that end-of-line comment without a line break at the end is allowed
5020                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
5021                x.setLeadingComment("// X"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5022                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
5023                assertTrue(x.getLeadingComment() == "// X"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5024                
5025                // check that end-of-line comment with embedded end of line 
5026                // not allowed
5027                try {
5028                        x.setLeadingComment("// X\n extra"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5029                        assertTrue(false);
5030                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
5031                        // pass
5032                }
5033                
5034        }

5098        /**
5099         * Exercise the client properties of a node.
5100         * 
5101         * @param x the node to test
5102         */
5103        void tClientProperties(ASTNode x) {
5104                
5105                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
5106                
5107                // a node initially has no properties
5108                assertTrue(x.properties().size() == 0);
5109                assertTrue(x.getProperty("1") == null); //$NON-NLS-1$
5110 
5111                // clearing an unset property does not add it to list of known ones
5112                x.setProperty("1", null); //$NON-NLS-1$
5113                assertTrue(x.getProperty("1") == null); //$NON-NLS-1$
5114                assertTrue(x.properties().size() == 0);
5115 
5116                // setting an unset property does add it to the list of known ones
5117                x.setProperty("1", "a1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5118                assertTrue(x.getProperty("1") == "a1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5119                assertTrue(x.properties().size() == 1);
5120                Map.Entry[] m = (Map.Entry[]) x.properties().entrySet().toArray(new Map.Entry[1]);
5121                assertTrue(m[0].getKey() == "1"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5122                assertTrue(m[0].getValue() == "a1"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5123 
5124                // setting an already set property just changes its value
5125                x.setProperty("1", "a2"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5126                assertTrue(x.getProperty("1") == "a2"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5127                assertTrue(x.properties().size() == 1);
5128                m = (Map.Entry[]) x.properties().entrySet().toArray(new Map.Entry[1]);
5129                assertTrue(m[0].getKey() == "1"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5130                assertTrue(m[0].getValue() == "a2"); //$NON-NLS-1$
5131 
5132                // clearing a set property removes it from list of known ones
5133                x.setProperty("1", null); //$NON-NLS-1$
5134                assertTrue(x.getProperty("1") == null); //$NON-NLS-1$
5135                assertTrue(x.properties().size() == 0);
5136                
5137                
5138                // ========= test 2 and 3 properties
5139                x.setProperty("1", "a1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5140                x.setProperty("2", "b1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5141                x.setProperty("3", "c1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5142                assertTrue(x.getProperty("1") == "a1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5143                assertTrue(x.getProperty("2") == "b1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5144                assertTrue(x.getProperty("3") == "c1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5145                assertTrue(x.properties().size() == 3);
5146                assertTrue(x.properties().get("1") == "a1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5147                assertTrue(x.properties().get("2") == "b1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5148                assertTrue(x.properties().get("3") == "c1"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5149                x.setProperty("1", "a2"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5150                x.setProperty("2", "b2"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$
5151                x.setProperty("3", "c2"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$

5204                        public ASTNode wrap() {

5564        /**
5565         * Walks the given AST and assigns properly-nested (but otherwise totally bogus)
5566         * source ranges to all nodes.
5567         */
5568        void assignSourceRanges(ASTNode target) {
5569                final StringBuffer buffer = new StringBuffer();
5570                final List stack = new ArrayList();
5571                // pretend that every construct begins with "(" and ends with ")"
5572                class PositionAssigner extends ASTVisitor {
5573                        PositionAssigner() {
5574                                // visit Javadoc.tags();
5575                                super(true);
5576                        }
5577                        public void preVisit(ASTNode node) {
5578                                int start = buffer.length();
5579                                buffer.append("(");
5580                                // push start position - popped by postVisit for same node
5581                                stack.add(new Integer(start));
5582                        }
5583                        public void postVisit(ASTNode node) {
5584                                // pop start position placed there by preVisit
5585                                int start = ((Integer) stack.remove(stack.size() - 1)).intValue();
5586                                buffer.append(")");
5587                                int length = buffer.length() - start;
5588                                node.setSourceRange(start, length);
5589                        }
5590                }
5591                target.accept(new PositionAssigner());
5592        }
5593        
5594        public void testClone() {
5595                ASTNode x = SampleASTs.oneOfEach(ast);
5596                assignSourceRanges(x);
5597                assertTrue(x.subtreeMatch(new CheckPositionsMatcher(), x));
5598                
5599                // same AST clone
5600                ASTNode y = ASTNode.copySubtree(ast, x);
5601                assertTrue(x.subtreeMatch(new CheckPositionsMatcher(), y));
5602                assertTrue(y.subtreeMatch(new CheckPositionsMatcher(), x));
5603                
5604                // different AST clone
5605                AST newAST = AST.newAST(ast.apiLevel());
5606                ASTNode z = ASTNode.copySubtree(newAST, x);
5607                assertTrue(x.subtreeMatch(new CheckPositionsMatcher(), z));
5608                assertTrue(z.subtreeMatch(new CheckPositionsMatcher(), x));
5609        }
5610

6403        public void testPrefixExpression() {
6404                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
6405                final PrefixExpression x = ast.newPrefixExpression();
6406                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
6407                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
6408                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
6409                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
6410                assertTrue(x.getOperand().getParent() == x);
6411                assertTrue(x.getOperator() != null);
6412                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.PREFIX_EXPRESSION);
6413                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == 
6414                        PrefixExpression.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
6415                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
6416                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
6417                
6418                // Operator property - mandatory typesafe enumeration
6419                // check the names of the operators
6420                assertTrue(PrefixExpression.Operator.INCREMENT.toString().equals("++")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6421                assertTrue(PrefixExpression.Operator.DECREMENT.toString().equals("--")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6422                assertTrue(PrefixExpression.Operator.PLUS.toString().equals("+")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6423                assertTrue(PrefixExpression.Operator.MINUS.toString().equals("-")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6424                assertTrue(PrefixExpression.Operator.COMPLEMENT.toString().equals("~")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6425                assertTrue(PrefixExpression.Operator.NOT.toString().equals("!")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6426                
6427                PrefixExpression.Operator[] known = {
6428                        PrefixExpression.Operator.INCREMENT,
6429                        PrefixExpression.Operator.DECREMENT,
6430                        PrefixExpression.Operator.PLUS,
6431                        PrefixExpression.Operator.MINUS,
6432                        PrefixExpression.Operator.COMPLEMENT,
6433                        PrefixExpression.Operator.NOT,
6434                };
6435                
6436                // check all operators are distinct
6437                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
6438                        for (int j = 0; j < known.length; j++) {
6439                                assertTrue(i == j || !known[i].equals(known[j]));
6440                        }
6441                }
6442 
6443                // check all operators work
6444                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
6445                        previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
6446                        x.setOperator(known[i]);
6447                        assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
6448                        assertTrue(x.getOperator().equals(known[i]));
6449                }
6450                // ensure null does not work as an operator
6451                try {
6452                        x.setOperator(null);
6453                        assertTrue(false);
6454                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
6455                        // pass
6456                }
6457 
6458                // check toOperator lookup of operator by name
6459                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
6460                        String name = known[i].toString();
6461                        assertTrue(PrefixExpression.Operator.toOperator(name).equals(known[i]));
6462                }
6463                assertTrue(PrefixExpression.Operator.toOperator("huh") == null); //$NON-NLS-1$
6464
