6571        public void testInfixExpression() {
6572                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
6573                final InfixExpression x = ast.newInfixExpression();
6574                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
6575                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
6576                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
6577                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
6578                assertTrue(x.getLeftOperand().getParent() == x);
6579                assertTrue(x.getOperator() != null);
6580                assertTrue(x.getRightOperand().getParent() == x);
6581                assertTrue(x.extendedOperands().isEmpty());
6582                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.INFIX_EXPRESSION);
6583                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == 
6584                        InfixExpression.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
6585                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
6586                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
6587                
6588                // Operator property - mandatory typesafe enumeration
6589                // check the names of the operators
6590                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.TIMES.toString().equals("*")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6591                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.DIVIDE.toString().equals("/")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6592                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.REMAINDER.toString().equals("%")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6593                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.PLUS.toString().equals("+")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6594                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.MINUS.toString().equals("-")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6595                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.LEFT_SHIFT.toString().equals("<<")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6596                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.RIGHT_SHIFT_SIGNED.toString().equals(">>")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6597                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.RIGHT_SHIFT_UNSIGNED.toString().equals(">>>")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6598                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.LESS.toString().equals("<")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6599                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.GREATER.toString().equals(">")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6600                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.LESS_EQUALS.toString().equals("<=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6601                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.GREATER_EQUALS.toString().equals(">=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6602                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.EQUALS.toString().equals("==")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6603                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.NOT_EQUALS.toString().equals("!=")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6604                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.XOR.toString().equals("^")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6605                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.OR.toString().equals("|")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6606                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.AND.toString().equals("&")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6607                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.CONDITIONAL_OR.toString().equals("||")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6608                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.CONDITIONAL_AND.toString().equals("&&")); //$NON-NLS-1$
6609                
6610                InfixExpression.Operator[] known = {
6611                                InfixExpression.Operator.TIMES,
6612                                InfixExpression.Operator.DIVIDE,
6613                                InfixExpression.Operator.REMAINDER,
6614                                InfixExpression.Operator.PLUS,
6615                                InfixExpression.Operator.MINUS,
6616                                InfixExpression.Operator.LEFT_SHIFT,
6617                                InfixExpression.Operator.RIGHT_SHIFT_SIGNED,
6618                                InfixExpression.Operator.RIGHT_SHIFT_UNSIGNED,
6619                                InfixExpression.Operator.LESS,
6620                                InfixExpression.Operator.GREATER,
6621                                InfixExpression.Operator.LESS_EQUALS,
6622                                InfixExpression.Operator.GREATER_EQUALS,
6623                                InfixExpression.Operator.EQUALS,
6624                                InfixExpression.Operator.NOT_EQUALS,
6625                                InfixExpression.Operator.XOR,
6626                                InfixExpression.Operator.OR,
6627                                InfixExpression.Operator.AND,
6628                                InfixExpression.Operator.CONDITIONAL_OR,
6629                                InfixExpression.Operator.CONDITIONAL_AND,
6630                };
6631                
6632                // check all operators are distinct
6633                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
6634                        for (int j = 0; j < known.length; j++) {
6635                                assertTrue(i == j || !known[i].equals(known[j]));
6636                        }
6637                }
6638 
6639                // check all operators work
6640                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
6641                        previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
6642                        x.setOperator(known[i]);
6643                        assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
6644                        assertTrue(x.getOperator().equals(known[i]));
6645                }
6646                // ensure null does not work as an operator
6647                try {
6648                        x.setOperator(null);
6649                        assertTrue(false);
6650                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
6651                        // pass
6652                }
6653 
6654                // check toOperator lookup of operator by name
6655                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
6656                        String name = known[i].toString();
6657                        assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.toOperator(name).equals(known[i]));
6658                }
6659                assertTrue(InfixExpression.Operator.toOperator("huh") == null); //$NON-NLS-1$

7312        /** @deprecated using deprecated code */
7313        public void testModifiers() {
7314                
7315                // check all modifiers match their JVM spec values
7316                assertTrue(Modifier.ABSTRACT == 0x0400);
7317                assertTrue(Modifier.FINAL == 0x0010);
7318                assertTrue(Modifier.NATIVE == 0x0100);
7319                assertTrue(Modifier.NONE == 0x0000);
7320                assertTrue(Modifier.PRIVATE == 0x0002);
7321                assertTrue(Modifier.PROTECTED == 0x0004);
7322                assertTrue(Modifier.PUBLIC == 0x0001);
7323                assertTrue(Modifier.STATIC == 0x0008);
7324                assertTrue(Modifier.STRICTFP == 0x0800);
7325                assertTrue(Modifier.SYNCHRONIZED == 0x0020);
7326                assertTrue(Modifier.TRANSIENT == 0x0080);
7327                assertTrue(Modifier.VOLATILE == 0x0040);
7328                
7329                // check that all
7330                final int[] mods =
7331                        {
7332                                Modifier.ABSTRACT,
7333                                Modifier.FINAL,
7334                                Modifier.NATIVE,
7335                                Modifier.PRIVATE,
7336                                Modifier.PROTECTED,
7337                                Modifier.PUBLIC,
7338                                Modifier.STATIC,
7339                                Modifier.STRICTFP,
7340                                Modifier.SYNCHRONIZED,
7341                                Modifier.TRANSIENT,
7342                                Modifier.VOLATILE,
7343                                };
7344                                
7345                for (int i=0; i< mods.length; i++) {
7346                        int m = mods[i];
7347                        assertTrue(Modifier.isAbstract(m) == (m == Modifier.ABSTRACT));
7348                        assertTrue(Modifier.isFinal(m) == (m == Modifier.FINAL));
7349                        assertTrue(Modifier.isNative(m) == (m == Modifier.NATIVE));
7350                        assertTrue(Modifier.isPrivate(m) == (m == Modifier.PRIVATE));
7351                        assertTrue(Modifier.isProtected(m) == (m == Modifier.PROTECTED));
7352                        assertTrue(Modifier.isPublic(m) == (m == Modifier.PUBLIC));
7353                        assertTrue(Modifier.isStatic(m) == (m == Modifier.STATIC));
7354                        assertTrue(Modifier.isStrictfp(m) == (m == Modifier.STRICTFP));
7355                        assertTrue(Modifier.isSynchronized(m) == (m == Modifier.SYNCHRONIZED));
7356                        assertTrue(Modifier.isTransient(m) == (m == Modifier.TRANSIENT));
7357                        assertTrue(Modifier.isVolatile(m) == (m == Modifier.VOLATILE));
7358                }
7359                
7360                if (ast.apiLevel() == AST.JLS2) {
7361                        // node type introduced in 3.0 API
7362                        try {
7363                                ast.newModifier(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD);
7364                                assertTrue(false);
7365                        } catch (UnsupportedOperationException e) {
7366                                // pass
7367                        }
7368                        try {
7369                                ast.newModifiers(Modifier.NONE);
7370                                assertTrue(false);
7371                        } catch (UnsupportedOperationException e) {
7372                                // pass
7373                        }
7374                        // skip rest of tests
7375                        return;
7376                }
7377                
7378                // JLS3 only
7379                long previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
7380                final Modifier x = ast.newModifier(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD);
7381                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
7382                previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
7383                assertTrue(x.getAST() == ast);
7384                assertTrue(x.getParent() == null);
7385                assertTrue(x.getKeyword() == Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD);
7386                assertTrue(x.getNodeType() == ASTNode.MODIFIER);
7387                assertTrue(x.structuralPropertiesForType() == 
7388                        Modifier.propertyDescriptors(ast.apiLevel()));
7389                // make sure that reading did not change modification count
7390                assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() == previousCount);
7391                
7392                // ModifierKeyword property - mandatory typesafe enumeration
7393                // check the names of the modifiers
7394                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD.toString().equals("public")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7395                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PROTECTED_KEYWORD.toString().equals("protected")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7396                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PRIVATE_KEYWORD.toString().equals("private")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7397                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STATIC_KEYWORD.toString().equals("static")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7398                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.ABSTRACT_KEYWORD.toString().equals("abstract")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7399                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.FINAL_KEYWORD.toString().equals("final")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7400                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.SYNCHRONIZED_KEYWORD.toString().equals("synchronized")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7401                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.NATIVE_KEYWORD.toString().equals("native")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7402                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.TRANSIENT_KEYWORD.toString().equals("transient")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7403                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.VOLATILE_KEYWORD.toString().equals("volatile")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7404                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STRICTFP_KEYWORD.toString().equals("strictfp")); //$NON-NLS-1$
7405 
7406                final Modifier.ModifierKeyword[] known = {
7407                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD,
7408                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PROTECTED_KEYWORD,
7409                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PRIVATE_KEYWORD,
7410                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STATIC_KEYWORD,
7411                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.ABSTRACT_KEYWORD,
7412                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.FINAL_KEYWORD,
7413                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.SYNCHRONIZED_KEYWORD,
7414                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.NATIVE_KEYWORD,
7415                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.TRANSIENT_KEYWORD,
7416                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.VOLATILE_KEYWORD,
7417                        Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STRICTFP_KEYWORD,
7418                };
7419                
7420                // check all modifiers are distinct
7421                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
7422                        for (int j = 0; j < known.length; j++) {
7423                                assertTrue(i == j || !known[i].equals(known[j]));
7424                        }
7425                }
7426 
7427                // check all modifiers work
7428                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
7429                        previousCount = ast.modificationCount();
7430                        x.setKeyword(known[i]);
7431                        assertTrue(ast.modificationCount() > previousCount);
7432                        assertTrue(x.getKeyword().equals(known[i]));
7433                }
7434                // ensure null does not work as an operator
7435                try {
7436                        x.setKeyword(null);
7437                        assertTrue(false);
7438                } catch (RuntimeException e) {
7439                        // pass
7440                }
7441 
7442                // check toKeyword lookup of modifier by name
7443                for (int i = 0; i < known.length; i++) {
7444                        String name = known[i].toString();
7445                        assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.toKeyword(name).equals(known[i]));
7446                }
7447                assertTrue(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.toKeyword("huh") == null); //$NON-NLS-1$
7448 
7449                // check AST.newModifiers(flags)
7450                for (int i = 0; i < mods.length; i++) {
7451                        int m = mods[i];
7452                        List result = ast.newModifiers(m);
7453                        assertEquals(1, result.size());
7454                        Modifier modNode = (Modifier) result.get(0);
7455                        assertEquals(m, modNode.getKeyword().toFlagValue());
7456                }
7457                
7458                // check AST.newModifiers ordering
7459                final Modifier.ModifierKeyword[] expectedOrder = {
7460                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD,
7461                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PROTECTED_KEYWORD,
7462                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PRIVATE_KEYWORD,
7463                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.ABSTRACT_KEYWORD,
7464                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STATIC_KEYWORD,
7465                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.FINAL_KEYWORD,
7466                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.SYNCHRONIZED_KEYWORD,
7467                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.NATIVE_KEYWORD,
7468                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STRICTFP_KEYWORD,
7469                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.TRANSIENT_KEYWORD,
7470                                Modifier.ModifierKeyword.VOLATILE_KEYWORD,
7471                        };
7472                int all = 0;
7473                for (int i = 0; i < mods.length; i++) {
7474                        all |= mods[i];
7475                }
7476                List result = ast.newModifiers(all);
7477                assertEquals(expectedOrder.length, result.size());
7478                for (int i = 0; i< expectedOrder.length; i++) {
7479                        final Modifier modifier = ((Modifier) result.get(i));
7480                        assertEquals(expectedOrder[i], modifier.getKeyword());
7481                        if (modifier.isAbstract()) {
7482                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.ABSTRACT_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7483                        } else if (modifier.isFinal()) {
7484                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.FINAL_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7485                        } else if (modifier.isNative()) {
7486                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.NATIVE_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7487                        } else if (modifier.isPrivate()) {
7488                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PRIVATE_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7489                        } else if (modifier.isProtected()) {
7490                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PROTECTED_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7491                        } else if (modifier.isPublic()) {
7492                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.PUBLIC_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7493                        } else if (modifier.isStatic()) {
7494                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STATIC_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7495                        } else if (modifier.isStrictfp()) {
7496                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.STRICTFP_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7497                        } else if (modifier.isSynchronized()) {
7498                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.SYNCHRONIZED_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7499                        } else if (modifier.isTransient()) {
7500                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.TRANSIENT_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7501                        } else {
7502                                assertEquals(Modifier.ModifierKeyword.VOLATILE_KEYWORD, modifier.getKeyword());
7503                        } 
7504                }
7505        }
7506                
7507        public void testSubtreeBytes() {
7508                ASTNode x = SampleASTs.oneOfEach(ast);
7509                final int subtreeBytes = x.subtreeBytes();
7510                assertTrue(subtreeBytes > 0);
7511        }
